## Terabit systems advantage
[Previous](https://www.terabitsystems.com/#%20)[Pause](https://www.terabitsystems.com/#%20)[Next](https://www.terabitsystems.com/#%20)
Industry leading Customer Service
Cost Recovery Specialists
Bullet Proof Warranty
Terabit Systems is more than a supplier of top-quality networking hardware. We are a customer-centered business that strives to provide you the best, hassle-free customer service in the network hardware industry. It’s simple, you have enough going on managing your day to day network operations. The experience of buying hardware should not be something you dread. You will enjoy working with our San Francisco-based Networking Specialists and look at buying networking hardware in a whole new light.
In addition to the savings you receive buying refurbished equipment, we also help extend your budget with our asset recovery/hardware re-marketing services. If you have surplus gear or are switching platforms, we can help lower your total cost of ownership by buying your unused or used networking equipment and offering fair-market value or trade-in on your new networking equipment. Give us a call to set up a free audit of your gear.
We make purchasing networking hardware simple for you. If anything goes wrong within the first year, we will replace it or offer a full refund. Simple enough? Our rigorous testing procedures allow us to certify our equipment with rock solid warranties. Our tight shipping process ensures it arrives safely – on time.

# Arista
[live chat application](http://www.livechatinc.com/?partner=lc_1051108)
### We specialize in high performance switching solutions.
**Arista Networks** offers great networking solutions – across 1/10/40 and 100GbE products - for large data center and high-performance computing environments such as high-frequency trading (HFT). Arista Networks was recently noted in Gartner’s Magic Quadrant for data center networking. 
Check out Arista’s low latency [switches](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista/7100-series) and connect with Terabit Systems at +1 (415) 230-4353 or [send us an email.](http://info.terabitsystems.com/quote-me-network-hardware)

## Terabit systems advantage
[Previous](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista/700/710p720x/ccs-710p#%20)[Pause](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista/700/710p720x/ccs-710p#%20)[Next](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista/700/710p720x/ccs-710p#%20)
Industry leading Customer Service
Cost Recovery Specialists
Bullet Proof Warranty
Terabit Systems is more than a supplier of top-quality networking hardware. We are a customer-centered business that strives to provide you the best, hassle-free customer service in the network hardware industry. It’s simple, you have enough going on managing your day to day network operations. The experience of buying hardware should not be something you dread. You will enjoy working with our San Francisco-based Networking Specialists and look at buying networking hardware in a whole new light.
In addition to the savings you receive buying refurbished equipment, we also help extend your budget with our asset recovery/hardware re-marketing services. If you have surplus gear or are switching platforms, we can help lower your total cost of ownership by buying your unused or used networking equipment and offering fair-market value or trade-in on your new networking equipment. Give us a call to set up a free audit of your gear.
We make purchasing networking hardware simple for you. If anything goes wrong within the first year, we will replace it or offer a full refund. Simple enough? Our rigorous testing procedures allow us to certify our equipment with rock solid warranties. Our tight shipping process ensures it arrives safely – on time.

# Products
[![](https://www.terabitsystems.com/sites/default/files/Selection_117.png?1574063023)](https://www.terabitsystems.com/juniper) Juniper Networks offers a high performing line of edge and core routing designed to meet the needs of the most demanding carrier- and provider-class installations. Network Operators especially appreciate JunOS (the Juniper Operating System) for its granular optimization and customization characteristics. Terabit Systems is an independent reseller, not associted with Juniper Networks. [View All Juniper Products](https://www.terabitsystems.com/juniper) |  [![](https://www.terabitsystems.com/sites/default/files/arista.jpg?1443639109)](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista) Arista Networks delivers software driven cloud networking solutions for large data center and high-performance computing environments. With more than two million cloud networking ports being deployed worldwide, Arista delivers a portfolio of 1/10/40 and 100GbE products that redefine network architectures, bring extensibility to networking, and dramatically change the price/performance of data center networks. [View All Arista Products](https://www.terabitsystems.com/arista) |  [![](https://www.terabitsystems.com/sites/default/files/brocade_0.png?1396424198)](https://www.terabitsystems.com/brocade) When you need cost-effective and reliable routing, switching and storage products for campus, enterprise and branch settings, turn to Brocade. Brocade has a proven track record working with the world’s largest IT organizations and specializes in offering flexible, “pay as you grow” port licensing combined with unique stacking architecture that can handle today’s most demanding IT environments. [View All Brocade Products](https://www.terabitsystems.com/brocade)  
---|---|---  
[![](https://www.terabitsystems.com/sites/default/files/cisco.png?1396424136)](https://www.terabitsystems.com/cisco-systems) Cisco has become synonymous with network hardware by providing specific products for specific needs and situations. As with IBM, no one has ever been fired for buying Cisco. Ubiquitous, familiar, reliable. Raul, our in-house Cisco expert, is here to answer all your Cisco questions. Give us a call today! [View All Cisco Products](https://www.terabitsystems.com/cisco-systems) |  |
